<div>
<div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Sensient Technologies Corporation</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Reports Results for the Quarter Ended June 30, 2015</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Reported EPS from Continuing Operations Increased to 64 Cents from 62 Cents in the Second Quarter of 2014</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Adjusted EPS is 80 Cents in the Quarter</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Foreign Currency Translation Reduced Reported EPS by 11% and Adjusted EPS by 9%</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">MILWAUKEE&#8212;July 23, 2015 <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">&#8212;</font> Sensient Technologies Corporation (NYSE: SXT) reported earnings per share from continuing operations of 64 cents in the second quarter of 2015 compared to 62 cents in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; Revenue was $346.0 million in this year&#8217;s second quarter compared to $373.4 million in the comparable period last year.&#160; Operating income was $45.1 million in the second quarter of 2015 compared to $49.7 million in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; The consolidated operating margin was 13.0% in the quarter compared to 13.3% in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; Foreign currency translation had a significant impact on the second quarter results, reducing reported revenue by 8%, operating income by 9%, and earnings per share by 11%.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">In 2014, Sensient initiated a restructuring plan to eliminate underperforming operations, consolidate manufacturing facilities, and improve operational efficiencies within the Company.&#160; The restructuring costs related to this plan are included in the reported results. Restructuring and other costs reduced operating income by $10.5 million, or 17 cents per share, in this year&#8217;s second quarter and $11.6 million, or 20 cents per share, in the second quarter of 2014.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center">- MORE -</div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The adjusted results, discussed below, eliminate the impact of restructuring and other&#160;costs and enhance the overall understanding of the Company&#8217;s performance. Sensient&#8217;s second quarter adjusted earnings per share were 80 cents compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter adjusted earnings per share of 81 cents. Adjusted operating income was $55.5 million and $61.3 million in the second quarters of 2015 and 2014, respectively. Foreign currency translation reduced adjusted operating income by 7.3% and adjusted earnings per share by 8.6%.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">For the six months ended June 30, 2015, reported earnings per share from continuing operations were $1.28 compared to 66 cents per share in last year&#8217;s comparable period.&#160; Revenue was $692.2 million in the first half of 2015 compared to $740.5 million in the first six months of 2014.&#160; Operating income from continuing operations was $91.5 million and $58.3 million in the first six months of 2015 and 2014, respectively.&#160; Foreign currency translation reduced revenue by 8% and operating income by 14% in the first half of 2015.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">For the six months ended June 30, 2015, adjusted earnings per share from continuing operations were $1.56 compared to $1.53 in the first six months of 2014.&#160; Adjusted operating income was $109.1 million and $116.1 million for the first six months of 2015 and 2014, respectively.&#160; Foreign currency translation reduced adjusted operating income by 7.0% and adjusted earnings per share by 7.8% for the year to date period.&#160; Restructuring and other costs reduced operating income by $17.6 million, or 28 cents per share, in the first half of 2015 and $57.8 million, or 86 cents per share, in the comparable period last year.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Cash provided by operating activities was $46.3 million in the second quarter compared to $49.6 million in the second quarter of 2014.&#160; The decrease was driven by the impact of foreign exchange rates and higher restructuring payments, which were partially offset by working capital improvements.&#160; In the first six months of 2015, cash provided by operating activities has increased over 10% from last year&#8217;s comparable period. The increase is primarily driven by improvements in working capital.&#160; The Company continued to repurchase shares in the second quarter, and in total, the Company has repurchased 1.9 million shares of its common stock this year.&#160; Including dividend payments, the Company has returned more than $140 million to shareholders through June 30<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">th</sup> of this year.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#8220;The second quarter results showed solid performances by many of our operations,&#8221; said Paul Manning, President and CEO of Sensient Technologies Corporation.&#160; &#8220;Most of the businesses in both the Color Group and the Flavors &amp; Fragrances Group delivered solid profit growth.&#160; Our strategy is working and Sensient is moving in a positive direction.&#8221;</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">BUSINESS REVIEW</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">The Color Group reported revenue of $119.3 million in the quarter compared to $132.2 million in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; Operating income was $24.8 million in the second quarter compared to $30.7 million in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; Foreign currency continued to have a significant impact, reducing both revenue and operating income by approximately 10% in the quarter.&#160; Most of the Color Group&#8217;s businesses performed well in the second quarter.&#160; In local currency, the food and beverage colors and cosmetic colors businesses reported mid-single digit revenue growth, and the pharmaceutical colors business reported double-digit revenue and profit growth.&#160; Favorable results from these businesses were more than offset by the results from the&#160;specialty inks&#160;business, which was affected by unfavorable currency impacts, soft demand and other operational issues.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">For the first six months of 2015, Color Group revenue was $239.9 million compared to $265.2 million in the comparable period last year.&#160; Operating income was $50.9 million for the first six months of 2015 compared to $60.5 million in the first six months of 2014. Foreign currency translation has had a significant impact on both revenue and operating income, reducing both by over 9% in the first six months of 2015.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">The Flavors &amp; Fragrances Group reported second quarter revenue of $204.6 million compared to $217.5 million reported in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; Operating income was $32.5 million compared to $34.1 million in last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; The Flavors &amp; Fragrances Group&#8217;s operating margin was 15.9% in the quarter as several business units reported solid local currency operating profit growth; including North America Beverage, BioNutrients, Savory Europe, Fragrances and Natural Ingredients.&#160; Foreign currency translation reduced both revenue and operating income in the second quarter, by 8% and 4%, respectively.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">The Flavors &amp; Fragrances Group reported revenue of $410.6 million and $431.8 million in the first six months of 2015 and 2014, respectively.&#160; Operating income was $63.0 million and $64.4 million in the first six months of 2015 and 2014, respectively.&#160; Foreign currency translation reduced both revenue and operating income in the first six months of 2015, by 7% and 3%, respectively.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">The Corporate &amp; Other segment, which includes the Company&#8217;s operations in Asia Pacific, reported revenue of $33.9 million and $35.4 million in the second quarters of 2015 and 2014, respectively.&#160; For the six months ended June 30, 2015, revenue was $65.5 million compared to $67.6 million reported in the first six months of last year.&#160; Foreign currency translation reduced revenue by 5% and 4%, respectively, in the current quarter and first six months of 2015.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">2015 OUTLOOK</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.3pt">Sensient is maintaining its previous adjusted earnings per share guidance to be within the range of $3.00 and $3.09.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">ABOUT SENSIENT TECHNOLOGIES</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 22.5pt">Sensient Technologies Corporation is a leading global manufacturer and marketer of colors, flavors and fragrances.&#160; Sensient employs advanced technologies at facilities around the world to develop specialty food and beverage systems, cosmetic and pharmaceutical systems, inkjet and specialty inks and colors, and other specialty and fine chemicals.&#160; The Company&#8217;s customers include major international manufacturers representing most of the world&#8217;s best-known brands.&#160; Sensient is headquartered in Milwaukee, Wisconsin.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left">Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Amounts</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">The Company's 2015 results from continuing operations include pre-tax restructuring and other charges of $10.5 million ($7.7 million after-tax or $0.17 per share) and $17.6 million ($13.2 million after-tax or $0.28 per share) for the three and six month periods ended June 30, 2015, respectively, related to eliminating underperforming operations, consolidating manufacturing facilities, improving efficiencies within the Company and other items.&#160; The Company's 2014 results from continuing operations include pre-tax restructuring and other charges of $11.6 million ($9.7 million after-tax or $0.20 per share) and $57.8 million ($42.8 million after-tax or $0.86 per share) for the three and six month periods ended June 30, 2014.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">These non-GAAP financial measures are utilized by management in comparing our operating performance on a consistent basis. We believe that these financial measures are appropriate to enhance an overall understanding of our underlying operating performance trends compared to historical and prospective periods. Management also believes that these measures are useful to investors in their analysis of our results of operations and provide improved comparability between fiscal periods. Non-GAAP financial measures should not be considered in isolation from, or as a substitute for, financial information calculated in accordance with GAAP. Investors are encouraged to review the reconciliation of these non-GAAP measures to their most directly comparable GAAP financial measures.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">Beginning in the first quarter of 2015, the results of operations for the Company&#8217;s businesses in Central and South America, previously reported in the Corporate &amp; Other segment, are now reported in the Flavors &amp; Fragrances segment. Results for 2014 have been restated to reflect these changes. The 2015 and 2014 restructuring and other costs related to continuing operations are reported in the Corporate &amp; Other segment.</div>
